(the &#8220;Company&#8221;) issued a press release announcing financial results for the fiscal quarter ended May&#160;31, 2021 and related matters. A copy of this press release is furnished as Exhibit 99.1 hereto and is incorporated in this Item 2.02 by reference. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The information in this Item 2.02, including the exhibit attached hereto, and the information under Item 7.01 below, shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section. This information shall not be deemed to be incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference to such disclosure in this Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> in such a filing. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Item</span>&#160;<span style="text-decoration:underline">7.01</span>. <span style="text-decoration:underline">Regulation FD Disclosure</span>. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On July&#160;1, 2021, the Company is conducting a conference call and webcast beginning at 8:30 a.m. Eastern time regarding its results for the fiscal quarter ended May&#160;31, 2021 and related matters. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Slides prepared for the purposes of the conference call are available on the Company&#8217;s investor relations website at http://investor.walgreensbootsalliance.com. A link to the conference call will be available on the Company&#8217;s investor relations website at: http://investor.walgreensbootsalliance.com. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold"><span style="text-decoration:underline">Item</span><span style="text-decoration:underline">&#160;</span><span style="text-decoration:underline">9.01</span>. <span style="text-decoration:underline">Financial Statements and Exhibits</span>. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) <span style="text-decoration:underline">Exhibits</span> </p> <p style="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

an increase of 10.7&nbsp;percent on a reported basis and up 9.9&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Additional highlights </I></P>

</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Fiscal 2021 outlook </I></P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Company raised guidance to around 10&nbsp;percent growth in constant currency adjusted EPS from continuing operations
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">DEERFIELD, Ill., July&nbsp;1, 2021 - Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. (Nasdaq: WBA) today announced financial results for the third quarter of
fiscal 2021, which ended May&nbsp;31, 2021. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Chief Executive Officer Rosalind Brewer said, &#147;This quarter&#146;s results demonstrate continued momentum, and
while challenges lie ahead, we are in a strong position to grow and innovate our core retail and pharmacy businesses for the future. We are accelerating our investments to advance our operational excellence, including technology innovations that
support mass personalization, pharmacy of the future and the next phase of growth in tech-enabled healthcare. These investments are fueled by our Alliance Healthcare divestiture. I remain proud of our team members and the essential role they are
playing to help end the pandemic as the communities we serve continue to turn to our trusted brands and expert pharmacists.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Completion of Strategic
Transaction with AmerisourceBergen&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA completed the divestiture of the Alliance Healthcare businesses to AmerisourceBergen for a total
consideration of $6.5&nbsp;billion, made up of $6.275&nbsp;billion in cash (subject to a customary net cash and working capital adjustment, which will result in an additional net cash inflow of approximately $0.3 billion) and 2&nbsp;million shares
of AmerisourceBergen common stock. The company has used a portion of the proceeds to eliminate $3.3 </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">
billion in debt from its balance sheet and will deploy the remainder to accelerate growth of its core retail pharmacy and healthcare businesses. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Overview of Third Quarter Results </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA third quarter sales from continuing
operations increased 12.1&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $34.0&nbsp;billion, an increase of 10.4&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>,
reflecting strong growth in the International segment, aided by the formation of the company&#146;s joint venture in Germany during the fiscal year, and solid growth in the United States segment. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating income from continuing operations was $1.1&nbsp;billion in the third quarter, compared with a loss of $1.7&nbsp;billion in the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, primarily due to $2&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charges in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter related to goodwill and
intangible assets in Boots UK. Adjusted operating income from continuing operations increased 82.9&nbsp;percent on a reported currency basis to $1.5&nbsp;billion, an increase of 82.4&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. The increases reflect
strong adjusted gross profit growth across both pharmacy and retail in the United States and a rebound in International segment sales and profitability due to less severe <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> restrictions in the UK. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Total net earnings attributable to WBA were $1.2&nbsp;billion compared with a loss of $1.7&nbsp;billion in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter,
reflecting <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charges in the previous period, increased operating income in both segments and earnings from the company&#146;s equity method investment related to Option Care Health; this was
partially offset by a higher effective tax rate driven by discrete items in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Total adjusted net earnings in constant currency increased 79.5&nbsp;percent to $1.3&nbsp;billion. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Total EPS<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2 </SUP>in the third quarter was $1.38, compared with a loss of $1.95 in the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Total adjusted EPS increased 83.4&nbsp;percent to $1.51, up 81.4&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Net earnings from continuing operations in the third quarter were $1.1&nbsp;billion, up from a loss of $1.8&nbsp;billion in the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted net earnings from continuing operations increased 93.1&nbsp;percent to $1.2&nbsp;billion, up 91.6&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis compared with the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">EPS from continuing operations was $1.27 compared with a loss of $2.05 in the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted EPS from continuing operations was $1.38 compared with $0.71 the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting an increase of 93.6&nbsp;percent on a constant
currency basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Net cash provided by operating activities was $1.8&nbsp;billion in the third quarter and free cash flow was $1.4&nbsp;billion, a $788&nbsp;million
increase compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Overview of Fiscal 2021 <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Year-to-Date</FONT></FONT> Results </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Sales from continuing operations in the first nine months of fiscal 2021 increased
7.2&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period to $98.2&nbsp;billion, an increase of 6.1&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating income from continuing operations in the first nine months of fiscal 2021 increased $1.1&nbsp;billion from the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period to $1.4&nbsp;billion, with the $2&nbsp;billion in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charges in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period partially
offset by a $1.5&nbsp;billion charge from the company&#146;s equity earnings in AmerisourceBergen in the first quarter of fiscal 2021. Adjusted operating income from continuing operations in the first nine months of the fiscal year was
$3.9&nbsp;billion, an increase of 4.2&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period on a reported basis, up 3.9&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">For the first nine months of fiscal 2021, total net earnings attributable to WBA were $1.9&nbsp;billion, compared with $83&nbsp;million in the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period. Total adjusted net earnings in constant currency increased 8.0&nbsp;percent to $3.6&nbsp;billion. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#aaaaaa">2 </FONT></P>

</DIV></Center>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Total EPS<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>, including discontinued operations, was $2.21, up from
$0.09 at the same time last year. Total adjusted EPS increased 11.2&nbsp;percent to $4.13, up 10.3&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Net earnings from
continuing operations were $1.6&nbsp;billion, compared with a loss of $157&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period. Adjusted net earnings from continuing operations increased 8.4&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period, to $3.2&nbsp;billion, up 7.6&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">EPS from continuing operations for the
first nine months of fiscal 2021 increased to $1.89, compared with a loss of $0.18 in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period. Adjusted EPS from continuing operations was $3.74, an increase of 10.7&nbsp;percent on a reported
basis and an increase of 9.9&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Net cash provided by operating activities was $4.3&nbsp;billion in the first nine months of
fiscal 2021, an increase of $912&nbsp;million from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period, and free cash flow was $3.3&nbsp;billion, an increase of $873&nbsp;million from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
period. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Company Outlook </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The company raised fiscal 2021 guidance from <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-to-high</FONT></FONT> single digit growth to around 10&nbsp;percent growth in constant currency adjusted EPS from continuing operations. The revised guidance reflects strong results in
the third quarter and greater clarity on the impact of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccinations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Fighting the Pandemic </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Walgreens and Boots UK pharmacists continue to play a critical role on the front lines of the pandemic, including the following examples through June. </P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt"><B>Driving the Transformational Cost Management Program </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="16%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top"><FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE:95%">&#9675;</FONT></SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">The company is on track to deliver in excess of $2&nbsp;billion in annual cost savings by fiscal 2022.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Business Segments </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>United States: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The United States segment had third quarter sales of $28.7&nbsp;billion, an increase of 5.1&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
quarter. Comparable sales increased 6.4&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter reflecting an 8.4&nbsp;percent increase in comparable pharmacy sales and a 1.7&nbsp;percent increase in comparable retail sales.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Within comparable sales, prescriptions filled in the third quarter increased 9.8&nbsp;percent from a year earlier, including a positive impact of approximately 600
basis points from <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccinations. Total prescriptions filled in the quarter increased 8.7&nbsp;percent to 312.1&nbsp;million, including immunizations, adjusted to
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalents. Pharmacy sales, which accounted for 75.7&nbsp;percent of the segment&#146;s sales in the quarter, increased 6.3&nbsp;percent compared with the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Retail sales increased 1.4&nbsp;percent in the third quarter compared with the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, including adverse impacts from the store optimization programs. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Comparable retail sales increased
1.7&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting mass personalization and strength in beauty and photo aided by improved traffic trends. Comparable retail sales excluding tobacco and <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-cigarettes</FONT> increased 2.6&nbsp;percent. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Gross profit increased 15.5&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter and adjusted gross profit increased 14.5&nbsp;percent, in both cases reflecting strong sales growth, favorable retail margin due to product mix and improved pharmacy margin entirely due to product
mix from <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccinations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Third quarter SG&amp;A decreased by 0.4&nbsp;percent, and adjusted SG&amp;A increased by
6.5&nbsp;percent, primarily driven by a negative impact of approximately 500 basis points from <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> related costs, mainly related to the vaccination program, as well as higher growth investments, partially
offset by cost savings related to the Transformational Cost Management Program. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating income in the third quarter increased to $1.2&nbsp;billion compared with
$528&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted operating income increased 50.3&nbsp;percent, to $1.5&nbsp;billion, reflecting strong adjusted gross profit across both pharmacy and retail, partly offset by
significant costs related to the vaccination program and higher growth investments. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>International: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The International segment had third quarter sales of $5.3&nbsp;billion, an increase of 75.8&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
quarter, including a favorable currency impact of 17.1&nbsp;percent. Sales increased 58.7&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, which includes the impact of the company&#146;s wholesale joint venture in Germany, which was consolidated as of
November 2020. Excluding incremental sales from the joint venture, International segment sales on a constant currency basis increased 12.1&nbsp;percent, reflecting a partial recovery in the UK market as
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> restrictions were eased. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#aaaaaa">4 </FONT></P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Boots UK comparable pharmacy sales increased 3.7&nbsp;percent compared with the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting stronger pharmacy services and favorable timing of NHS reimbursement, partially offset by lower prescription volume. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Boots UK comparable retail sales increased 38.7&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Footfall on the high street
showed early signs of recovery amid a partial easing of strict lockdown measures, though travel locations in airports and train stations continued to face challenges. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Boots.com continued to perform strongly, with sales growth of 42.3&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Gross profit increased 55.0&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, including a favorable currency impact of
16.3&nbsp;percent. Adjusted gross profit increased 38.6&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting the ongoing recovery in UK retail sales. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">SG&amp;A in
the quarter decreased 63.9&nbsp;percent from the prior year quarter to $1.0&nbsp;billion, including an adverse currency impact of 3.8&nbsp;percent and the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charges in the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. On a constant currency basis, adjusted SG&amp;A increased 5.2&nbsp;percent, due entirely to the higher SG&amp;A associated with the formation of the Germany joint venture. Excluding the Germany
joint venture impact, both SG&amp;A and adjusted SG&amp;A decreased, reflecting cost savings from the Transformational Cost Management Program. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating income,
including a favorable currency impact of 0.1&nbsp;percent, was $36&nbsp;million compared with a loss of $2.2&nbsp;billion, which was primarily a result of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charges. Adjusted operating
income was $94&nbsp;million, an increase of $222&nbsp;million on a constant currency basis compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting less severe UK <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT>
restrictions, Boots.com performance and cost management actions. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Conference Call </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA will hold a conference call to discuss the third quarter results beginning at 8:30 a.m. Eastern time today, July&nbsp;1, 2021. The conference call will be simulcast
through the WBA investor relations website at: <FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" COLOR="#0000ff"><U>http://investor.walgreensbootsalliance.com</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL">. A replay of the conference call will be archived
on the website for 12 months after the call. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The replay also will be available from 11:30 a.m. Eastern time, July&nbsp;1 through July&nbsp;8, 2021, by

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Notes to Editors: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>About Walgreens Boots Alliance </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Walgreens Boots Alliance (Nasdaq: WBA) is a
global leader in retail pharmacy, impacting millions of lives every day through dispensing medicines, and providing accessible, high-quality care. With more than 170 years of trusted healthcare heritage and innovation in community pharmacy, the
company is meeting customers&#146; and patients&#146; needs through its convenient retail locations, digital platforms and health and beauty products. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Including
equity method investments, WBA has a presence in more than 25 countries, employs more than 450,000 people and has more than 21,000 stores. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA&#146;s purpose is to
help people across the world lead healthier and happier lives. The company is proud of its contributions to healthy communities, a healthy planet, an inclusive workplace and a sustainable marketplace. WBA is a Participant of the United Nations
Global Compact and adheres to its principles-based approach to responsible business. WBA is included in FORTUNE&#146;s 2021 list of the World&#146;s Most Admired Companies.* This is the 28th consecutive year that WBA or its predecessor company,
Walgreen Co., has been named to the list </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">More company information is available at
<FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" COLOR="#0000ff"><U>www.walgreensbootsalliance.com</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL">. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL">*&copy; 2021,

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>WALGREENS BOOTS ALLIANCE, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>SUPPLEMENTAL INFORMATION (UNAUDITED) </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>REGARDING <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> FINANCIAL MEASURES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">(in millions, except per share amounts) </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The following information
provides reconciliations of the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, as defined under SEC rules, presented in this press release to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented
in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles in the United States (GAAP). The company has provided the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures in the press release, which are not calculated or presented in
accordance with GAAP, as supplemental information and in addition to the financial measures that are calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP. Please refer to the notes to the &#147;Net Earnings and Diluted Net Earnings (Loss) Per
Share&#148; reconciliation table on page 14 for definitions of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures and related adjustments presented in this press release. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">These supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures are presented because management has evaluated the company&#146;s financial
results both including and excluding the adjusted items or the effects of foreign currency translation, as applicable, and believes that the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented provide
additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the company&#146;s business from period to period and trends in the company&#146;s historical operating results. These supplemental
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures should not be considered superior to, as a substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented in the press
release. The company does not provide a reconciliation for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> estimates on a forward-looking basis (including the information under &#147;Company Outlook&#148; above) where it is unable to provide a
meaningful or accurate calculation or estimation of reconciling items and the information is not available without unreasonable effort. This is due to the inherent difficulty of forecasting the timing or amount of various items that have not yet
occurred, are out of the company&#146;s control and/or cannot be reasonably predicted, and that would impact diluted net earnings per share, the most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP financial measure. For the same reasons, the company is
unable to address the probable significance of the unavailable information. Forward-looking <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provided without the most directly comparable GAAP financial measures may vary materially
from the corresponding GAAP financial measures. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Constant currency </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The
company also presents certain information related to current period operating results in &#147;constant currency,&#148; which is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. These amounts are calculated by translating
current period results at the foreign currency exchange rates used in the comparable period in the prior year. The company presents such constant currency financial information because it has significant operations outside of the United States
reporting in currencies other than the U.S. dollar and this presentation provides a framework to assess how its business performed excluding the impact of foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Comparable sales </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">For the company&#146;s United States and International
segments, comparable sales are defined as sales from stores that have been open for at least 12 consecutive months without closure for seven or more consecutive days, including due to looting or store damage, and without a major remodel or being
subject to a natural disaster in the past 12 months as well as <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-commerce</FONT> sales. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">E-commerce</FONT> sales include digitally initiated sales online or through mobile
applications. Relocated stores are not included as comparable stores for the first 12 months after the relocation. Acquired stores are not included as comparable sales for the first 12 months after acquisition or conversion, when applicable,
whichever is later. Comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales, comparable retail sales, comparable number of prescriptions and comparable number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions refer to total sales,
pharmacy sales, retail sales, number of prescriptions and number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions, respectively. Comparable retail sales for previous periods have been restated to include <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-commerce</FONT> sales. The method of calculating comparable sales varies across the retail industry. As a result, the company&#146;s method of calculating comparable sales may not be the same as other retailers&#146;
methods. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#aaaaaa">11 </FONT></P>


</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">With respect to the International segment, comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales and comparable retail sales,
are presented on a constant currency basis, which is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. Refer to the discussion above in &#147;Constant currency&#148; for further details on constant currency calculations. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Key Performance Indicators </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The company considers certain metrics, including
all comparable metrics, number of prescriptions, number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions and number of locations at period end, to be key performance indicators because the company&#146;s management has
evaluated its results of operations using these metrics and believes that these key performance indicators presented provide additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the company from period to period and
trends in its historical operating results. These key performance indicators should not be considered superior to, as a substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented
herein. These measures may not be comparable to similarly-titled performance indicators used by other companies. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#aaaaaa">12 </FONT></P>


</DIV></Center>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to equity earnings (loss) in AmerisourceBergen consist of the Company&#146;s proportionate share of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments reported by AmerisourceBergen consistent with the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. The Company recognized equity losses in AmerisourceBergen of
$1,373&nbsp;million during the three months ended November&nbsp;30, 2020. These equity losses are primarily due to AmerisourceBergen recognition of $5.6&nbsp;billion, net of tax, charges related to its ongoing opioid litigation in its financial
statements for the three months period ended September&nbsp;30, 2020. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related amortization includes amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets and inventory valuation
adjustments. Amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets includes amortization of intangibles assets such as customer relationships, trade names, trademarks and contract intangibles. Intangible asset amortization excluded from the related <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure represents the entire amount recorded within the company&#146;s GAAP financial statements. The revenue generated by the associated intangible assets has not been excluded from the related <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. Amortization expense, unlike the related revenue, is not affected by operations of any particular period unless an intangible asset becomes impaired or the estimated useful life of an intangible
asset is revised. These charges are primarily recorded within selling, general and administrative expenses. Business combination accounting principles require us to measure acquired inventory at fair value. The fair value of the inventory reflects
cost of acquired inventory and a portion of the expected profit margin. The acquisition-related inventory valuation adjustments excludes the expected profit margin component from cost of sales recorded under the business combination accounting
principles. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Transformational Cost Management Program and Store Optimization Program charges are costs associated with a formal
restructuring plan. These charges are primarily recorded within selling, general and administrative expenses. These costs do not reflect current operating performance and are impacted by the timing of restructuring activity. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">4</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Certain legal and regulatory accruals and settlements relate to significant charges associated with certain legal
proceedings. The Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance because it does not incur such charges on a predictable basis and exclusion of such charges enables more consistent evaluation of the Company&#146;s operating
performance. These charges are recorded within selling, general and administrative expenses. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">5</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">The company&#146;s United States segment inventory is accounted for using the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">last-in-first-out</FONT></FONT></FONT> (&#147;LIFO&#148;) method. This adjustment represents the impact on cost of sales as if the United States segment inventory is accounted for using <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-in</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-out</FONT> (&#147;FIFO&#148;) method. The LIFO provision is affected by changes in inventory quantities, product mix, and manufacturer pricing practices, which may be
impacted by market and other external influences. Therefore, the company cannot control the amounts recognized or timing of these items. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">6</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related costs are transaction and integration costs associated with certain merger, acquisition and
divestitures related activities. These costs include all charges incurred on certain mergers, acquisition and divestitures related activities, for example, including costs related to integration efforts for successful merger, acquisition and
divestitures activities. These charges are primarily recorded within selling, general and administrative expenses. These costs are significantly impacted by the timing and complexity of the underlying merger, acquisition and divestitures related
activities and do not reflect the Company&#146;s current operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">7</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Gain or loss on certain derivative instruments used as economic hedges of the company&#146;s net investments in foreign
subsidiaries. These charges are recorded within other income (expense). We do not believe this volatility related to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> adjustment on the underlying
derivative instruments reflects the company&#146;s operational performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Includes significant gain on sale of equity method investment. During the three and nine months ended May&nbsp;31, 2021,
the Company recorded a gain of $98&nbsp;million and $290&nbsp;million respectively, in Other income due to a partial sale of ownership interests in Option Care Health by the Company&#146;s equity method investee HC Group Holdings.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">9</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to income tax provision include adjustments to the GAAP basis tax provision commensurate with <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments and certain discrete tax items including U.S. tax law changes and equity method <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> tax. These charges are recorded within income tax provision
(benefit). </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">10</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to post tax equity earnings from other equity method investments consist of the proportionate share of certain
equity method investees&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> items or unusual or infrequent items consistent with the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments. These charges are recorded within
post tax earnings (loss) from other equity method investments. Although the Company may have shareholder rights and board representation commensurate with its ownership interests in these equity method investees, adjustments relating to equity
method investments are not intended to imply that the Company has direct control over their operations and resulting revenue and expenses. Moreover, these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures have limitations in that
they do not reflect all revenue and expenses of these equity method investees. In the three months ended May&nbsp;31, 2021 due to partial sales of ownership interests in Option Care Health, our equity method investee HC Group Holdings lost the
ability to control Option Care Health and, therefore, deconsolidated Option Care Health in its financial statements. As a result of this deconsolidation, HC Group Holdings recognized a gain of $1.2&nbsp;billion and the Company recorded its share of
equity earnings in HC Group Holdings of $576&nbsp;million during the three months ended May&nbsp;31, 2021. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Loss on early extinguishment of debt related to the Company&#146;s cash tender offers to partially purchase and retire
$3.3&nbsp;billion of long term U.S. denominated notes. The Company excludes these charges to enable a more consistent evaluation of the Company&#146;s financial performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">12</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Goodwill and intangible assets arising from acquisition related activities are recorded by the Company following the
analysis to determine the fair value of consideration paid and the assignment of fair values to all tangible and intangible assets acquired. Impairment of goodwill and intangible assets do not relate to the ordinary course of the Company&#146;s
business. The Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance because it does not incur such charges on a predictable basis and exclusion of such charges enables more consistent evaluation of the Company&#146;s operating
performance. These charges are recorded within selling, general and administrative expenses. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">13</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Store damage and inventory losses as a result of looting in the U.S., net of insurance recoveries. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">14</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Due to the anti-dilutive effect resulting from the reported net loss, the impact of potentially dilutive securities on the
per share amounts has been omitted from the quarterly calculation of weighted-average common shares outstanding for diluted EPS for the three and nine months ended May&nbsp;31, 2020. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

for adjusted diluted net earnings per common share calculation purposes for the three and nine months ended May&nbsp;31, 2020. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Operating income (loss) for United States includes equity earnings (loss) in AmerisourceBergen. As a result of the two
month reporting lag, operating income (loss) for the three and nine month period ended May&nbsp;31, 2021 includes AmerisourceBergen equity earnings (loss) for the period of January&nbsp;1, 2021 through March&nbsp;31, 2021 and the period of
July&nbsp;1, 2020 through March&nbsp;31, 2021, respectively. Operating income (loss) for the three and nine month period ended May&nbsp;31, 2020 includes AmerisourceBergen equity earnings for the period of January&nbsp;1, 2020 through March&nbsp;31,
2020, and the period of July&nbsp;1, 2019 through March&nbsp;31, 2020, respectively. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Operating margins and adjusted operating margins have been calculated excluding equity earnings (loss) in
AmerisourceBergen and adjusted equity earnings (loss) in AmerisourceBergen, respectively. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Free cash flow is defined as net cash provided by operating activities in a period less additions to property, plant and
equipment (capital expenditures) made in that period.&nbsp;This measure does not represent residual cash flows available for discretionary expenditures as the measure does not deduct the payments required for debt service and other contractual
obligations or payments for future business acquisitions. Therefore, we believe it is important to view free cash flow as a measure that provides supplemental information to our entire statements of cash flows. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
